563
NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
 
My son V.K. Thulasi Krishnaa, aged 13 Years who is mentally retarded (Autism), son of R. Vijendran born on
6th November 2005, residing at No.7, S2, 3rd Main Road, 9th Cross Street, Dhandeeswaram Nagar, Velachery,
Chennai-600 042, Tamil Nadu shall henceforth be known as V. THULASI KRISHNAA.
Chennai, 
R. VIJENDRAN
4th January 2019.
